\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00065}00065    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} lg, size, wasted\_pages;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00066}00066    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} kAlignShift = 3;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00069}00069    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} kPageShift = 12;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00071}00071   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} next\_class = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00072}00072   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} alignshift = kAlignShift;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00077}00077     size\_shift[lg] = kAlignShift;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00078}00078   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00079}00079 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00080}00080   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (size = kAlignment; size <= kMaxSize; size += (1 << alignshift)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00081}00081     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} lg = stb\_log2\_floor(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00082}00082     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (lg > last\_lg) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00083}00083       \textcolor{comment}{// Increase alignment every so often.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00084}00084       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00085}00085       \textcolor{comment}{// Since we double the alignment every time size doubles and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00086}00086       \textcolor{comment}{// size >= 128, this means that space wasted due to alignment is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00087}00087       \textcolor{comment}{// at most 16/128 i.e., 12.5\%.  Plus we cap the alignment at 256}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00088}00088       \textcolor{comment}{// bytes, so the space wasted as a percentage starts falling for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00089}00089       \textcolor{comment}{// sizes > 2K.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00090}00090       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((lg >= 7) \&\& (alignshift < 8)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00091}00091         alignshift++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00092}00092       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00093}00093       size\_base[lg] = next\_class -\/ ((size-\/1) >> alignshift);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00094}00094       size\_shift[lg] = alignshift;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00095}00095     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00096}00096 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00097}00097     class\_to\_size[next\_class] = size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00098}00098     last\_lg = lg;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00099}00099 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00100}00100     next\_class++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00101}00101   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00102}00102 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00103}00103   \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the number of pages we should allocate to split into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00104}00104   \textcolor{comment}{// small objects for a given class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00105}00105   wasted\_pages = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00106}00106   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (cl = 1; cl < next\_class; cl++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00107}00107     \textcolor{comment}{// Allocate enough pages so leftover is less than 1/8 of total.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00108}00108     \textcolor{comment}{// This bounds wasted space to at most 12.5\%.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00109}00109     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} psize = kPageSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00110}00110     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} s = class\_to\_size[cl];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00111}00111     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((psize \% s) > (psize >> 3)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00112}00112       psize += kPageSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00113}00113     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00114}00114     class\_to\_pages[cl] = (int) (psize >> kPageShift);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00115}00115     wasted\_pages += (int) psize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb_8c_source_l00116}00116   \}}
